***kurgan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a> (64321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ĞºÑÑĞ³Ğ°ÌĞ½</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurgÃ¡n</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span></span> language (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kurgans</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A prehistoric burial mound once used by peoples in Siberia and Central Asia.
<ul><li><b>2004</b>, Benjamin Fortson, <i>Indo-European Language and Culture</i>, Blackwell, 2005, p. 41
<dl><dd>The <b>kurgans</b> and the burials they contain are consistent with the early <a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>Ie</a> burial practices outlined above, and the late Lithuanian archaeologist Marija Gimbutas proposed that the <a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a> peoples <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> in fact early Indo-Europeans.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Philip L. <a href = vnd.unilang:kohl.html>Kohl</a>, <i>Chapter 6: The Maikop Singularity: The Unequal Accumulation of Wealth on the Bronze Age Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:steppe.html>Steppe</a>?</i>, Bryan K. <a href = vnd.unilang:hanks.html>Hanks</a>, Katheryn M. Linduff (<a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>), <i>Social Complexity in Prehistoric Eurasia: Monuments, Metals and Mobility</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=fEK-BkqXfJACamp;pg=PA91amp;dq=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;f=false">page 91</a>,
<dl><dd>In 1897 N. I. Veselovskii excavated the very large, nearly 11 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> high Oshad <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b> or barrow in the town of Maikop in the Kuban region near the foothills of the northwestern Caucasus (the present-day capital of the Adygei Republic).<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>â¦<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>This discovery stimulated the excavation of other large <b>kurgans</b> located in the same general region, some of which seemed royal-like in their dimensions and, when not robbed in antiquity, in their materials.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, David W. Anthony, <i>The Horse, the Wheel, and Language: How Bronze-Age <a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>Riders</a> from the Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:steppes.html>Steppes</a> Shaped the Modern World</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=0FDqf415wqgCamp;pg=PA329amp;dq=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22kurgan%22%7C%22kurgans%22amp;f=false">page 329</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> in the middle Volga region some <b>kurgans</b> have central graves containing adult females, as at Krasnosamarskoe IV.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>â¦<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>The appearance of adult females in one out of five <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b> graves, including central graves, suggests that gender <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not the only factor that determined who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> buried under a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kurgan.html>kurgan</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">burial mound</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">barrow</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tumulus</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kurk.html>kurk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">cork</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekker.html>trekker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">puller</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense relating to rollercoasters derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">corkscrew</i>.

***kus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a> (1318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kussaz</i>. The older Dutch forms with -u- are <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> from the verb, those with -o- derive directly from the noun. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kuss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kiss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">kys</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kus.html>kusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***kussen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a> (1475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cussen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kussijanÄ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kussen.html>kussen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kiss, to give a kiss to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kuste.html>kuste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zachtjes.html>zachtjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wang.html>wang</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>kissed</b> him gently on the cheek.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to practice kissing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>Niemand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kust.html>kust</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Nobody <b>kisses</b> better than he.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cussin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cuisin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cussin</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwaal.html>kwaal</a> (17338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kwÄla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwÄlÅ</i>.

***kwab.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwab</a> (26609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quappe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quabbe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwab</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwabben.html>kwabben</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwabje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A weak, blubbery mass, notably:
<ol><li>of human or animal tissue, such as quivering flesh, or a brain lobe</li>
<li>of aquatic plants</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several eel <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a>:
<ol><li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Lota_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Lota vulgaris"><i>Lota <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></a></span> (burbot)</li>
<li><i>Zoarces viviparus</i> (viviparous blenny)</li>
<li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gaidropsarus_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gaidropsarus vulgaris"><i>Gaidropsarus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/three-bearded_rockling" class="extiw" title="w:three-bearded rockling">three-bearded rockling</a>, syn. <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Motella_tricirrata" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Motella tricirrata"><i>Motella tricirrata</i></a></span>)</li></ol></li></ol>

***kwalijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwalijk.html>kwalijk</a> (998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">qualike</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">qualic</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quaelick</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quaedelick</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwaad.html>kwaad</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">quelik</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">quelike</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">quÄdelike</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">quÄlike</i> (gt; West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">kwealik</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">barely, scarcely</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adverb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<ol><li>bad, undesirable</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quattel</i>, <span class="Latn" lang="dum">quattele</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kwahtila</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*kwahtila</i>.

***kwartier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwartier.html>kwartier</a> (3369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quartier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">quartier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">quartÄrius</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwartier.html>kwartier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwartieren.html>kwartieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwartiertje.html>kwartiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A quarter of an hour, i.e. 15 minutes.</li>
<li>The quarter(s) at (a) person(s)'s disposal to live in; one's living <a href = vnd.unilang:quarters.html>quarters</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now uncommon  outside names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A neighborhood, defined part of a town or city.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buurt.html>buurt</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A quarter of an heraldic field.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">genealogy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> heraldry<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> All of one's ancestors up to a specified degree, indicated by the maximum number of possible ancestors at a given level (2, 4, 8, 16, etc.), generally listed on a document; originally used for nobles whose <a href = vnd.unilang:coats.html>coats</a> of arms would be displayed on such a document.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated  outside names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A region.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">landstreek</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regio.html>regio</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:streek.html>streek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***kwast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwast.html>kwast</a> (16524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quast</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kwast.html>kwast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwastuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwast.html>kwast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwasten.html>kwasten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwastje.html>kwastje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tassel</li>
<li>fine-haired brush</li>
<li>knot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in wood</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">knoest</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">noest</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>weird and/or stuck-up person</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">squash</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lemonade or another citrus-based beverage; a <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> made of lemon juice, water and optionally sugar <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">can denote both cold and hot drinks</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwekerij.html>kwekerij</a> (43522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kweker.html>kweker</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwekerij.html>kwekerij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwekerijen.html>kwekerijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwekerij.html>kwekerijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A farm where plants are grown, in particular for saplings, flowers and fruits (including culinary vegetables), often without harvesting the entire plant unless it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a sapling.</li>
<li>A nursery where: <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suriname" class="extiw" title="w:Suriname">Suriname</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any animals are raised or <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fish, molluscs, arthropods or algae are raised or grown.</li>
<li>The activity of farming at a farm of one of the above <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>.</li></ol>

***kwetsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwetsen.html>kwetsen</a> (3735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quetsen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">quezzon</i>, of uncertain origin but compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">quetschen</i>. Early influence or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> borrowing of the Old Dutch term from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">quasser</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> proposed.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwetsen.html>kwetsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wound, to injure</li>
<li>to offend, to insult</li></ol>

***kwetsuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwetsuur.html>kwetsuur</a> (74810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwetsen.html>kwetsen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wound, injure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-uur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
